msg:This is a small hotel designed and run by a few young people. It met all my needs for a hotel or travel accommodation, and it also got an additional surprise that I didn't expect!
The design is very local, with thatched roofs, rammed loess walls, and dead branches cut into stoneware jars, giving it an eternal beauty. It is better to say that there are bananas planted in front of and behind the house than in a banana forest. Several rooms are more accurate.
The hot eye masks and hydrating masks prepared in the room are heart-warming.
The black forest cake in afternoon tea is neither sweet nor greasy, silky and refreshing.
The temperature of Good Night Milk includes the temperature itself and the pitted red dates slices inside.
When I walked in, I asked the security guy at the door if the sugar cane growing in the courtyard was sugar cane. When I left the room, there were two of them standing at the door.
When we checked out, we actually received a tangerine as a gift from the front desk. It has thin skin, juicy and sweet taste, which is better than all kinds of tangerines bought in the market. The nearby farmer uncle said he grew it himself and gave it to us.
The hotel has excellent design and exquisite decoration, but most people are cold-hearted. You have to check in and check out at the door. This hotel has a rare combination of exquisiteness and warmth!
Like üëç!

msg:A typical internet celebrity hotel, good for taking photos, but a bit awkward in terms of location, not far from the surrounding famous scenic spots and county towns, there are no natural landscapes around the hotel, just a tributary of the Zuojiang River. There are too many human factors in the park, basically it is a resort, it feels more suitable for people living in surrounding cities to come and relax, for those who come to Guangxi specifically for tourism, they still prefer the natural scenery of Guangxi.
The hotel has a complete range of facilities, and the afternoon tea is not bad, not the kind of deal with things. If you come here for tourism, it is recommended to go to the county town for meals, which is cheap, special and delicious.

About some issues: 1. Go to several other famous hotels in Chongzuo, basically they will contact you the day before to ask about your needs, and there will be a housekeeper to communicate in advance. Here is a housekeeper added after checking in.
2. When eating breakfast, I found some problems with the service. The main plate on the breakfast table was basically empty, and the things I ordered would not be served without urging. There was no order at all, and whoever urged would serve. The whole park eats breakfast in one place, and people are very messy, and even have to fight for seats.
3. Many bicycles in the park are broken, and the shuttle bus in the parking lot basically picks up luggage, and you can hardly see it at other times.
4. There is no privacy when staying, because guests can walk around the park, and the glass is transparent, so you can either choose to draw the curtains in the room to not see the scenery, or choose to let the passing guests see you
Summary: Only hardware, the software is not up to par, no flaws, but no nostalgia, just come here to check in and take pictures for the first time, and I may not stay here again when I come to Chongzuo.
